    "content": "```rust\n//! src/module_77.rs\n//! Hyper-parameter tuning utilities used by VisuTility Orchestrator\n//!\n//! This module demonstrates the Strategy, Factory, and Observer patterns\n//! to provide pluggable hyper-parameter tuning back-ends while emitting\n//! structured events that can be consumed by experiment trackers,\n//! dashboards, or automated re-training triggers.\n\nuse std::{\n    collections::HashMap,\n    fmt,\n    sync::{Arc, Mutex, Weak},\n    time::{Duration, Instant},\n};\n\nuse async_trait::async_trait;\nuse rand::{distributions::Uniform, prelude::*};\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\nuse thiserror::Error;\nuse tokio::task;\n\n/// Anything in the platform that wants to be informed about tuning progress\n/// implements this trait.  \n/// The Observer Pattern is implemented through a very small, allocation-free\n/// event bus (see `EventBus` below).\n#[async_trait]\npub trait TuningEventHandler: Send + Sync {\n    async fn on_event(&self, event: TuningEvent);\n}\n\n/// Enum of the events we produce while tuning.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum TuningEvent {\n    TrialStarted {\n        trial_id: usize,\n        parameters: HyperParams,\n    },\n    TrialCompleted {\n        trial_id: usize,\n        objective: f32,\n        duration: Duration,\n        parameters: HyperParams,\n    },\n    TuningFinished {\n        best_trial_id: usize,\n        best_objective: f32,\n        best_parameters: HyperParams,\n        total_duration: Duration,\n    },\n}\n\n/// Very small event bus\u2014thread-safe, allocation-friendly.\n///\n/// This could be swapped out for a fully-fledged pub/sub implementation\n/// (Kafka, NATS, Redis Stream, etc) but is intentionally lightweight.\n#[derive(Clone, Default)]\npub struct EventBus {\n    /// Vector of weak references so handlers can be dropped without\n    /// requiring explicit deregistration.\n    handlers: Arc<Mutex<Vec<Weak<dyn TuningEventHandler>>>>,\n}\n\nimpl EventBus {\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self::default()\n    }\n\n    pub fn subscribe(&self, handler: Arc<dyn TuningEventHandler>) {\n        self.handlers.lock().unwrap().push(Arc::downgrade(&handler));\n    }\n\n    async fn emit(&self, event: TuningEvent) {\n        let mut stale_handlers = Vec::new();\n\n        for (idx, handler_weak) in self.handlers.lock().unwrap().iter().enumerate() {\n            if let Some(handler_arc) = handler_weak.upgrade() {\n                handler_arc.on_event(event.clone()).await;\n            } else {\n                stale_handlers.push(idx);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Cleanup stale handlers\n        if !stale_handlers.is_empty() {\n            let mut handlers = self.handlers.lock().unwrap();\n            for idx in stale_handlers.into_iter().rev() {\n                handlers.swap_remove(idx);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Any tuner algorithm must implement this trait.\n/// Strategy Pattern: different tuning algorithms share the common interface.\n#[async_trait]\npub trait HyperparameterTuner: Send + Sync {\n    async fn tune(&mut self) -> Result<TuningSummary, TuningError>;\n}\n\n/// A summary of the tuning run\u2014serializable for experiment tracking.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct TuningSummary {\n    pub best_trial_id: usize,\n    pub best_objective: f32,\n    pub best_parameters: HyperParams,\n    pub trials_ran: usize,\n    pub total_time: Duration,\n}\n\n/// Commonly raised errors during hyper-parameter tuning.\n#[derive(Error, Debug)]\npub enum TuningError {\n    #[error(\"invalid configuration: {0}\")]\n    InvalidConfig(String),\n    #[error(\"I/O error: {0}\")]\n    Io(#[from] std::io::Error),\n    #[error(\"internal error: {0}\")]\n    Internal(String),\n}\n\n/// Enumerates the algorithms we support; can be serialized from config files.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum TuningAlgorithm {\n    RandomSearch,\n    GridSearch,\n    // Bayesian, HyperBand, etc. can be added here\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for TuningAlgorithm {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n        let text = match self {\n            TuningAlgorithm::RandomSearch => \"random_search\",\n            TuningAlgorithm::GridSearch => \"grid_search\",\n        };\n        write!(f, \"{text}\")\n    }\n}\n\n/// Range specification for a single hyper-parameter.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum HyperParamRange {\n    Continuous { min: f32, max: f32 },\n    Discrete { choices: Vec<f32> },\n}\n\nimpl HyperParamRange {\n    /// Sample one value uniformly from the range.\n    fn sample(&self, rng: &mut impl Rng) -> f32 {\n        match self {\n            HyperParamRange::Continuous { min, max } => {\n                rng.sample(Uniform::new_inclusive(*min, *max))\n            }\n            HyperParamRange::Discrete { choices } => {\n                let idx = rng.gen_range(0..choices.len());\n                choices[idx]\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Generate the full grid for grid-search algorithms.\n    fn full_grid(&self) -> Vec<f32> {\n        match self {\n            HyperParamRange::Continuous { min, max } => {\n                // For simplicity, break into 10 buckets\n                (0..=10)\n                    .map(|i| min + ((*max - *min) * i as f32 / 10.0))\n                    .collect()\n            }\n            HyperParamRange::Discrete { choices } => choices.clone(),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// A full set of hyper-parameters for one trial.  \n/// Using `serde_json::Value` would be more flexible but numeric values are\n/// enough for this example.\npub type HyperParams = HashMap<String, f32>;\n\n/// Tune-time configuration that can be read from YAML/JSON/Protobuf, etc.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct HyperparameterTuningConfig {\n    pub algorithm: TuningAlgorithm,\n    pub search_space: HashMap<String, HyperParamRange>,\n    pub max_trials: usize,\n}\n\n/// Factory Pattern: pick the correct strategy implementation at runtime.\npub struct TunerFactory;\n\nimpl TunerFactory {\n    pub fn build(\n        cfg: HyperparameterTuningConfig,\n        event_bus: EventBus,\n    ) -> Result<Box<dyn HyperparameterTuner>, TuningError> {\n        match cfg.algorithm {\n            TuningAlgorithm::RandomSearch => Ok(Box::new(RandomSearchTuner::new(cfg, event_bus))),\n            TuningAlgorithm::GridSearch => Ok(Box::new(GridSearchTuner::new(cfg, event_bus))),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/* --------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Random Search Implementation\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nstruct RandomSearchTuner {\n    cfg: HyperparameterTuningConfig,\n    event_bus: EventBus,\n    rng: ThreadRng,\n}\n\nimpl RandomSearchTuner {\n    fn new(cfg: HyperparameterTuningConfig, event_bus: EventBus) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            cfg,\n            event_bus,\n            rng: rand::thread_rng(),\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn sample_hyperparams(&mut self) -> HyperParams {\n        self.cfg\n            .search_space\n            .iter()\n            .map(|(k, v)| (k.clone(), v.sample(&mut self.rng)))\n            .collect()\n    }\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl HyperparameterTuner for RandomSearchTuner {\n    async fn tune(&mut self) -> Result<TuningSummary, TuningError> {\n        let start = Instant::now();\n        let mut best_objective = f32::MAX;\n        let mut best_trial_id = 0;\n        let mut best_params = HyperParams::new();\n\n        for trial_id in 0..self.cfg.max_trials {\n            let params = self.sample_hyperparams();\n            self.event_bus\n                .emit(TuningEvent::TrialStarted {\n                    trial_id,\n                    parameters: params.clone(),\n                })\n                .await;\n\n            // Run the expensive objective function in a separate task so the\n            // caller's async runtime remains responsive.\n            let params_clone = params.clone();\n            let obj_start = Instant::now();\n            let objective = task::spawn_blocking(move || mock_objective_fn(&params_clone))\n                .await\n                .map_err(|e| TuningError::Internal(e.to_string()))?;\n\n            let duration = obj_start.elapsed();\n\n            self.event_bus\n                .emit(TuningEvent::TrialCompleted {\n                    trial_id,\n                    objective,\n                    duration,\n                    parameters: params.clone(),\n                })\n                .await;\n\n            if objective < best_objective {\n                best_objective = objective;\n                best_trial_id = trial_id;\n                best_params = params;\n            }\n        }\n\n        let total_time = start.elapsed();\n        self.event_bus\n            .emit(TuningEvent::TuningFinished {\n                best_trial_id,\n                best_objective,\n                best_parameters: best_params.clone(),\n                total_duration: total_time,\n            })\n            .await;\n\n        Ok(TuningSummary {\n            best_trial_id,\n            best_objective,\n            best_parameters: best_params,\n            trials_ran: self.cfg.max_trials,\n            total_time,\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n/* --------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Grid Search Implementation\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nstruct GridSearchTuner {\n    cfg: HyperparameterTuningConfig,\n    event_bus: EventBus,\n    grid: Vec<HyperParams>,\n}\n\nimpl GridSearchTuner {\n    fn new(cfg: HyperparameterTuningConfig, event_bus: EventBus) -> Self {\n        let grid = build_grid(&cfg.search_space);\n        Self { cfg, event_bus, grid }\n    }\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl HyperparameterTuner for GridSearchTuner {\n    async fn tune(&mut self) -> Result<TuningSummary, TuningError> {\n        if self.grid.is_empty() {\n            return Err(TuningError::InvalidConfig(\n                \"Grid search produced zero combinations\".into(),\n            ));\n        }\n\n        let total_trials = self.cfg.max_trials.min(self.grid.len());\n        let start = Instant::now();\n        let mut best_objective = f32::MAX;\n        let mut best_trial_id = 0;\n        let mut best_params = HyperParams::new();\n\n        for trial_id in 0..total_trials {\n            let params = self.grid[trial_id].clone();\n\n            self.event_bus\n                .emit(TuningEvent::TrialStarted {\n                    trial_id,\n                    parameters: params.clone(),\n                })\n                .await;\n\n            let obj_start = Instant::now();\n            let objective = task::spawn_blocking(move || mock_objective_fn(&params))\n                .await\n                .map_err(|e| TuningError::Internal(e.to_string()))?;\n            let duration = obj_start.elapsed();\n\n            self.event_bus\n                .emit(TuningEvent::TrialCompleted {\n                    trial_id,\n                    objective,\n                    duration,\n                    parameters: params.clone(),\n                })\n                .await;\n\n            if objective < best_objective {\n                best_objective = objective;\n                best_trial_id = trial_id;\n                best_params = params.clone();\n            }\n        }\n\n        let total_time = start.elapsed();\n        self.event_bus\n            .emit(TuningEvent::TuningFinished {\n                best_trial_id,\n                best_objective,\n                best_parameters: best_params.clone(),\n                total_duration: total_time,\n            })\n            .await;\n\n        Ok(TuningSummary {\n            best_trial_id,\n            best_objective,\n            best_parameters: best_params,\n            trials_ran: total_trials,\n            total_time,\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n/* --------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Helper Functions\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/// Mock objective function\u2014replace with real model training + validation.\n/// Lower is better.\nfn mock_objective_fn(params: &HyperParams) -> f32 {\n    // Deterministic-ish \u201cobjective\u201d so unit tests can assert repeatably.\n    params.values().fold(0.0, |acc, v| acc + (v * v)).sqrt()\n}\n\n/// Build a Cartesian product of all parameter ranges.\n/// For large spaces consider lazy evaluation or iterators.\nfn build_grid(search_space: &HashMap<String, HyperParamRange>) -> Vec<HyperParams> {\n    fn cartesian(\n        keys: &[String],\n        search_space: &HashMap<String, HyperParamRange>,\n        idx: usize,\n        current: &mut HyperParams,\n        grid: &mut Vec<HyperParams>,\n    ) {\n        if idx == keys.len() {\n            grid.push(current.clone());\n            return;\n        }\n\n        let key = &keys[idx];\n        for val in search_space[key].full_grid() {\n            current.insert(key.clone(), val);\n            cartesian(keys, search_space, idx + 1, current, grid);\n        }\n        current.remove(key);\n    }\n\n    let keys: Vec<String> = search_space.keys().cloned().collect();\n    let mut grid = Vec::new();\n    let mut current = HyperParams::new();\n    cartesian(&keys, search_space, 0, &mut current, &mut grid);\n    grid\n}\n\n/* --------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Example Observer\u2014writes events to `tracing` & stdout\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nuse tracing::{info, Level};\nstruct LoggingObserver;\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl TuningEventHandler for LoggingObserver {\n    async fn on_event(&self, event: TuningEvent) {\n        info!(?event, \"tuning_event\");\n        // In a real implementation this could forward to Kafka, InfluxDB, etc.\n        println!(\"EVENT: {event:?}\");\n    }\n}\n\n/* --------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * When compiled as `cargo test` run a quick smoke test.\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use tracing_subscriber::FmtSubscriber;\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn test_random_search_smoke() {\n        // Enable logging for the observer\n        let subscriber = FmtSubscriber::builder().with_max_level(Level::INFO).finish();\n        let _ = tracing::subscriber::set_global_default(subscriber);\n\n        let mut space = HashMap::new();\n        space.insert(\n            \"lr\".into(),\n            HyperParamRange::Continuous { min: 0.0001, max: 0.1 },\n        );\n        space.insert(\n            \"dropout\".into(),\n            HyperParamRange::Discrete {\n                choices: vec![0.1, 0.2, 0.3],\n            },\n        );\n\n        let cfg = HyperparameterTuningConfig {\n            algorithm: TuningAlgorithm::RandomSearch,\n            search_space: space,\n            max_trials: 5,\n        };\n\n        let bus = EventBus::new();\n        bus.subscribe(Arc::new(LoggingObserver));\n\n        let mut tuner = TunerFactory::build(cfg, bus).unwrap();\n        let summary = tuner.tune().await.unwrap();\n\n        assert!(summary.trials_ran == 5);\n        assert!(summary.best_objective.is_finite());\n    }\n}\n```",

  }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl HyperparameterTuner for BayesianTuner {\n    fn strategy_name(&self) -> &'static str {\n        \"bayesian_search\"\n    }\n\n    fn tune(\n        &mut self,\n threshold_pct: f32,\n    tx_retrain: Sender<RetrainEvent>,\n    model_id: String,\n}\n\nimpl PerformanceMonitor {\n    /// Create a new monitor.\n    ///\n    /// * `window` \u2013 number of recent threshold_pct,\n            tx_retrain,\n            model_id,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Computes moving average loss over the internal window.\n    fn avg_loss(&self) -> Option<f32> {\n        if self.history.is_empty() {\n            return None;\n        }\n        Some(\n            self.history\n                .iter()\n                .map(|m| m.loss)\n                .sum::<f32>()\n                / self.history.len() as f32,\n        )\n    }\n}\n\nimpl MetricsObserver for PerformanceMonitor {\n    fn on_metrics_update(&mut self, metrics: &TrainingMetrics) {\n        // Maintain bounded window.\n        if self.history.len() == self.window {\n            self.history.pop_front();\n        }\n        self.history.push_back(*metrics);\n\n        // Compute rolling avg and detect degradation.\n        if let Some(avg_loss) = self.avg_loss() {\n            let worst_allowed = avg_loss * (1.0 + self.threshold_pct);\n            if metrics.loss > worst_allowed {\n degraded {:.2}% vs. rolling mean\",\n                        (metrics.loss / avg_loss - 1.0) * 100.0\n                    ),\n                };\n                // It's okay to ignore send errors {\n                    recv(self.rx_metrics) -> msg => {\n                        match msg {\n                            Ok((cfg, metrics)) => {\n                                // 1) Produce new config via tuner.\n                                let mut tuner = self.tuner.lock().expect(\"poisoned lock\");\n                                match tuner.tune(&cfg, &metrics) {\n                                    Ok(new_cfg) => {\n                                        // Send back to upstream training service\n                                        if let Err(err) = self.tx_config.send(new_cfg) {\n                                            eprintln!(\"TuningCoordinator: failed to send new config: {err}\");\n                                        }\n                                    }\n                                    Err(e) => eprintln!(\"TuningCoordinator: tune() failed: {e:?}\"),\n                                }\n\n                                // 2) Notify observers.\n                                for obs in self.observers.lock().expect(\"poisoned lock\").iter_mut() {\n                                    obs.on_metrics_update(&metrics);\n                                }\n                            }\n                            Err(_) => {\n                                // Upstream closed. Shutdown gracefully.\n                                break;\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                    recv(ticker) -> _ => {\n                        // Heart-beat for logging / metrics integration.\n                        // In prod we would emit metrics to Prometheus here.\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        });\n    }\n}\n\n//\n// ---------- Self-contained Integration Test -------------------------------------------------------\n//\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    #[test]\n    fn end_to_end_flow() {\n        // a) Wire channels.\n        let (tx_metrics, rx_metrics) = bounded::<(HyperParameterConfig, TrainingMetrics)>(4);\n        let (tx_cfg_out, rx_cfg_out) = bounded::<HyperParameterConfig>(4);\n        let (tx_retrain, _rx_retrain) = bounded::<RetrainEvent>(4);\n\n        // b) Concrete strategy + observer.\n        let tuner = TunerFactory::create(TunerKind::GridSearch);\n        let monitor = PerformanceMonitor::new(\"model-xyz\".into(), 4, 0.05, tx_retrain);\n\n        // c) Coordinator.\n        let coord = TuningCoordinator::new(tuner, vec![Box::new(monitor)], rx_metrics, tx_cfg_out);\n        coord.start();\n\n        // d) Push dummy metrics.\n        let mut cfg = HyperParameterConfig::new();\n        cfg.insert(\"lr\", 0.01);\n        cfg.insert(\"momentum\", 0.9);\n\n        for i in 0..5 {\n            let mut metrics = TrainingMetrics {\n                accuracy: 0.9,\n                f1_score: 0.92,\n                loss: 0.1 + i as f32 * 0.02,\n            };\n            tx_metrics.send((cfg.clone(), metrics)).unwrap();\n\n            // Receive tuned config.\n            let new_cfg = rx_cfg_out.recv().unwrap();\n            assert!(new_cfg.get(\"lr\").is_some());\n        }\n    }\n}\n```",

Model-Monitoring & Automated-Retraining Orchestrator\n//! --------------------------------------------------------------\n//! This module wires together the Observer & Strategy patterns used by the\n//! VisuTility Orchestrator to\n//!   1. observe live model-serving metrics,\n//!   2. detect statistical drift or performance regressions, and\n//!   3. trigger an automated retraining job through the internal MLOps\n//!      pipeline when necessary.\n//!\n//! It is fully self-contained and agnostic of the concrete metric backend,\n//! storage layer, or experiment-tracking implementation.  All of those\n//! concerns are injected via trait objects, keeping the module easily\n//! testable and reusable across binaries and workspaces.\n\nuse std::collections::VecDeque;\nuse std::sync::{Arc, Mutex};\nuse std::time::{Duration, Instant};\n\nuse log::{debug, error, info, warn};\nuse thiserror::Error;\n\n/// A normalized metric payload emitted by the Serving-Ops layer.\n///\n/// Requirements:\n///   \u2022 `value` MUST be normalized so that higher is always better.  \n///   \u2022 `timestamp` must be captured close to the model to guarantee\n///     time-series fidelity even in presence of network jitter.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct MetricSample {\n    pub metric_name: String,\n    pub value: f64,\n    pub timestamp: Instant,\n}\n\n/// Errors surfaced by the Model Monitor and its collaborators.\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum MonitorError {\n    #[error(\"observer failed: {0}\")]\n    ObserverFailure(String),\n    #[error(\"strategy evaluation failed: {0}\")]\n    StrategyFailure(String),\n}\n\n/// Trait implemented by components interested in real-time metric updates\n/// (dashboards, alarm systems, audit logs, \u2026).\npub trait MetricObserver: Send + Sync + 'static {\n    fn on_metric(&self, sample: &MetricSample) -> Result<(), MonitorError>;\n}\n\n/// Decision returned by a retraining strategy after evaluating a metric window.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq)]\npub enum RetrainingDecision {\n    NoAction,\n    ShouldRetrain,\n}\n\n/// Strategy that evaluates a sliding window of metrics and decides whether\n/// automated retraining should be triggered.\n///\n/// Implementations MUST be thread-safe and cheap to clone: they are wrapped\n/// in `Arc` internally.\npub trait RetrainingStrategy: Send + Sync + 'static {\n    fn evaluate(\n        &self,\n        metric_name: &str,\n        window: &[MetricSample],\n    ) -> Result<RetrainingDecision, MonitorError>;\n}\n\n/// A statistically-driven strategy that triggers retraining when the average\n/// of the last `window_size` samples drops below `min_acceptable_score`.\n///\n/// Example:\n///   For an F1-score in [0,1] you may want to trigger retraining once the\n///   average score of the last 10 samples falls under 0.80.\npub struct StatisticalAverageStrategy {\n    min_acceptable_score: f64,\n    window_size: usize,\n}\n\nimpl StatisticalAverageStrategy {\n    pub fn new(min_acceptable_score: f64, window_size: usize) -> Self {\n        assert!(\n            (0.0..=1.0).contains(&min_acceptable_score),\n            \"min_acceptable_score must be in [0,1]\"\n        );\n        assert!(window_size > 1, \"window_size must be > 1\");\n\n        Self {\n            min_acceptable_score,\n            window_size,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl RetrainingStrategy for StatisticalAverageStrategy {\n    fn evaluate(\n        &self,\n        _metric_name: &str,\n        window: &[MetricSample],\n    ) -> Result<RetrainingDecision, MonitorError> {\n        if window.len() < self.window_size {\n            return Ok(RetrainingDecision::NoAction);\n        }\n        let avg: f64 = window\n            .iter()\n            .rev()\n            .take(self.window_size)\n            .map(|s| s.value)\n            .sum::<f64>()\n            / self.window_size as f64;\n\n        debug!(\n            \"[Strategy::StatisticalAverage] avg={:.4} threshold={:.4}\",\n            avg, self.min_acceptable_score\n        );\n\n        if avg < self.min_acceptable_score {\n            Ok(RetrainingDecision::ShouldRetrain)\n        } else {\n            Ok(RetrainingDecision::NoAction)\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Central coordinator that\n///   \u2022 accumulates metric samples in a ring buffer,\n///   \u2022 notifies observers,\n///   \u2022 delegates to strategies for retraining decisions.\n///\n#[derive(Clone)]\npub struct ModelMonitor {\n    inner: Arc<Mutex<Inner>>,\n}\n\nstruct Inner {\n    window: VecDeque<MetricSample>,\n    max_window: usize,\n    observers: Vec<Arc<dyn MetricObserver>>,\n    strategies: Vec<Arc<dyn RetrainingStrategy>>,\n    cooldown: Duration,\n    last_retrain_at: Option<Instant>,\n}\n\nimpl ModelMonitor {\n    /// Create a new monitor.\n    ///\n    /// `max_window`  \u2013 maximum number of samples kept per metric  \n    /// `cooldown`    \u2013 minimum delay between two retraining triggers\n    pub fn new(max_window: usize, cooldown: Duration) -> Self {\n        assert!(max_window > 1, \"max_window must be > 1\");\n\n        Self {\n            inner: Arc::new(Mutex::new(Inner {\n                window: VecDeque::with_capacity(max_window),\n                max_window,\n                observers: Vec::new(),\n                strategies: Vec::new(),\n                cooldown,\n                last_retrain_at: None,\n            })),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Register a new observer.  Failures in an observer do not abort the\n    /// ingest flow; they are logged and swallowed.\n    pub fn register_observer<O>(&self, observer: O)\n    where\n        O: MetricObserver,\n    {\n        self.inner.lock().unwrap().observers.push(Arc::new(observer));\n    }\n\n    /// Register a new retraining strategy.  The first strategy voting for\n    /// `ShouldRetrain` short-circuits evaluation of further strategies.\n    pub fn register_strategy<S>(&self, strategy: S)\n    where\n        S: RetrainingStrategy,\n    {\n        self.inner.lock().unwrap().strategies.push(Arc::new(strategy));\n    }\n\n    /// Ingest a single metric sample into the monitor.\n    ///\n    /// Return `Ok(true)`  if a retraining event was emitted.  \n    /// Return `Ok(false)` if no action was taken.  \n    /// Return `Err(_)`    if a strategy returned an unrecoverable error.\n    pub fn ingest_metric(&self, sample: MetricSample) -> Result<bool, MonitorError> {\n        let mut inner = self.inner.lock().unwrap();\n\n        // 1) add sample to ring buffer\n        if inner.window.len() == inner.max_window {\n            inner.window.pop_front();\n        }\n        inner.window.push_back(sample.clone());\n\n        // 2) notify observers\n        for obs in &inner.observers {\n            if let Err(e) = obs.on_metric(&sample) {\n                error!(\"observer failed: {}\", e);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // 3) consult each strategy\n        for strategy in &inner.strategies {\n            match strategy.evaluate(&sample.metric_name, &inner.window) {\n                Ok(RetrainingDecision::ShouldRetrain) => {\n                    let now = Instant::now();\n                    if inner\n                        .last_retrain_at\n                        .map_or(true, |t| now.duration_since(t) >= inner.cooldown)\n                    {\n                        inner.last_retrain_at = Some(now);\n                        info!(\n                            \"Retraining triggered for metric '{}' (cooldown = {:?})\",\n                            sample.metric_name, inner.cooldown\n                        );\n                        return Ok(true);\n                    } else {\n                        warn!(\"Retraining skipped due to cooldown.\");\n                        return Ok(false);\n                    }\n                }\n                Ok(RetrainingDecision::NoAction) => {\n                    // continue with next strategy\n                }\n                Err(e) => return Err(e),\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok(false)\n    }\n}\n\n/// A trivial console observer handy for local debugging.\npub struct ConsoleObserver;\n\nimpl MetricObserver for ConsoleObserver {\n    fn on_metric(&self, sample: &MetricSample) -> Result<(), MonitorError> {\n        debug!(\n            \"[ConsoleObserver] metric={} value={:.4} ts={:?}\",\n            sample.metric_name, sample.value, sample.timestamp\n        );\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use std::thread;\n    use std::time::Duration;\n\n    struct CountingObserver {\n        counter: Arc<Mutex<u64>>,\n    }\n\n    impl CountingObserver {\n        fn new(counter: Arc<Mutex<u64>>) -> Self {\n            Self { counter }\n        }\n    }\n\n    impl MetricObserver for CountingObserver {\n        fn on_metric(&self, _sample: &MetricSample) -> Result<(), MonitorError> {\n            *self.counter.lock().unwrap() += 1;\n            Ok(())\n        }\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn retraining_is_triggered_when_average_drops() {\n        let monitor = ModelMonitor::new(10, Duration::from_secs(1));\n        monitor.register_strategy(StatisticalAverageStrategy::new(0.8, 5));\n\n        // push 5 good samples\n        for _ in 0..5 {\n            assert!(!monitor\n                .ingest_metric(MetricSample {\n                    metric_name: \"f1\".into(),\n                    value: 0.9,\n                    timestamp: Instant::now(),\n                })\n                .unwrap());\n        }\n\n        // push 5 degraded samples -> avg below threshold -> retrain\n        let mut triggered = false;\n        for _ in 0..5 {\n            triggered = monitor\n                .ingest_metric(MetricSample {\n                    metric_name: \"f1\".into(),\n                    value: 0.5,\n                    timestamp: Instant::now(),\n                })\n                .unwrap();\n        }\n        assert!(triggered);\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn observer_is_called_for_each_sample() {\n        let monitor = ModelMonitor::new(5, Duration::from_secs(60));\n        let counter = Arc::new(Mutex::new(0));\n        monitor.register_observer(CountingObserver::new(counter.clone()));\n\n        for _ in 0..3 {\n            monitor\n                .ingest_metric(MetricSample {\n                    metric_name: \"latency_ms\".into(),\n                    value: 15.0,\n                    timestamp: Instant::now(),\n                })\n                .unwrap();\n        }\n\n        assert_eq!(*counter.lock().unwrap(), 3);\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn cooldown_is_enforced_between_triggers() {\n        let monitor = ModelMonitor::new(10, Duration::from_millis(300));\n        monitor.register_strategy(StatisticalAverageStrategy::new(0.8, 1));\n\n        // first trigger should fire\n        assert!(monitor\n            .ingest_metric(MetricSample {\n                metric_name: \"accuracy\".into(),\n                value: 0.0,\n                timestamp: Instant::now(),\n            })\n            .unwrap());\n\n        // second trigger should be blocked by cooldown\n        assert!(!monitor\n            .ingest_metric(MetricSample {\n                metric_name: \"accuracy\".into(),\n                value: 0.0,\n                timestamp: Instant::now(),\n            })\n            .unwrap());\n\n        thread::sleep(Duration::from_millis(400));\n\n        // after cooldown passes, trigger should fire again\n        assert!(monitor\n            .ingest_metric(MetricSample {\n                metric_name: \"accuracy\".into(),\n                value: 0.0,\n                timestamp: Instant::now(),\n            })\n            .unwrap());\n    }\n}\n```",

They intentionally read like \u201cblack-box\u201d\n// contract tests: if an internal implementation detail changes, the tests\n// should still pass as long as the public API continues to satisfy its\n// documented behaviour.\n//\n// NOTE:  The production crate must expose the modules referenced below\n// (factory, registry, events, preprocessing, and model). timeout(max_wait, async {\n        loop {\n            if condition() {\n                return true;\n            }\n            tokio::time::sleep(Duration::from_millis(5)).await;\n        }\n    })\n    .await\n    .unwrap_or(false)\n}\n\n#[tokio::test]\nasync fn test_preprocessor_factory_resolves_expected_concrete_types() -> Result<()> {\n    // RGB\n    let rgb: Box<dyn Preprocessor> =\n        DataPreprocessorFactory::for_modality(SensorModality::Rgb)?;\n    assert_eq!(rgb.name(), \"RgbPreprocessor\");\n\n    // Thermal\n    let thermal: Box<dyn Preprocessor> =\n Core Component Identification\n\nThe experiment tracking functionality is distributed across multiple modules following a consistent architectural pattern:\n\n| Module | Primary Responsibility | Key Types |\n|--------|----------------------|-----------|\n| `module_12.txt` | In-memory experiment run management | `ExperimentTracker`, `ExperimentRun`, `TrainingEvent` |\n| `module_25.txt` | Tracker trait and factory | `ExperimentTracker` (trait), `FileTracker`, `HttpTracker`, `TrackerFactory` |\n| `module_20.txt` | Tracker trait and file-based logging | `ExperimentTracker` (trait), `LocalFileTracker`, `TrialFinishedEvent` |\n| `module_71.txt` | SQLite-backed persistence | `ExperimentTracker`, `ExperimentRecord` |\n| `module_55.txt` | Observer pattern for experiments | `ExperimentEvent`, `ExperimentObserver`, `TrialRecord` |\n| `module_48.txt` | JSONL file-based observer | `TuningObserver`, `JsonlTracker` |\n| `module_76.txt` | Monitoring integration | `ExperimentTracker` (for retraining logs) |\n\n### 2. Dependency Analysis\n\n#### Internal Dependencies (what core modules depend on):\n\n| Dependency | Modules Using It | Purpose |\n|------------|-----------------|---------|\n| `config.txt` | All trackers | `experiment_tracking_uri`, backend selection |\n| `utils.txt` | All modules | `AppConfig`, `event_bus`, error types, `ScopedTimer` |\n| `constants.txt` | Feature-flagged modules | `HYPERPARAM_TUNING` feature flag |\n| `serde`, `serde_json` | All trackers | Serialization of trials and metrics |\n| `tokio`, `async_trait` | Async trackers | Async I/O operations |\n| `rusqlite` | `module_71.txt` | SQLite persistence |\n| `reqwest` | `module_25.txt` | HTTP-based remote tracking |\n\n#### External Consumers (modules that use experiment tracking):\n\n| Consumer Module | How It Uses Experiment Tracking |\n|-----------------|--------------------------------|\n| `module_77.txt` | `EventBus` emits `TuningEvent` for experiment logging |\n| `module_54.txt` | `TuningCoordinator` feeds metrics to observers |\n| `module_43.txt` | `ModelMonitor` triggers retraining with metric logging |\n| `module_76.txt` | `RetrainTrigger` records experiments after tuning |\n| `module_20.txt` | `HyperparameterRunner` logs trials via tracker list |\n| `module_53.txt` | Tuning strategies log results |\n| `module_23.txt` | Factory creates tuners that integrate with trackers |\n\n### 3. Architectural Patterns Used\n\n1. **Strategy Pattern**: Multiple tuning algorithms (`GridSearchTuner`, `RandomSearchTuner`, `BayesianTuner`) implement common `Tuner`/`HyperparameterTuner` traits\n2. **Factory Pattern**: `TrackerFactory`, `TunerFactory` instantiate concrete implementations at runtime\n3. **Observer Pattern**: `ExperimentObserver`, `TrainingObserver`, `TuningObserver` receive notifications about trial events\n4. **Repository Pattern**: `ExperimentTracker` abstracts persistence (file, HTTP, SQLite backends)\n\n## Proposed Service API\n\n### RESTful API Design for Experiment Tracking Microservice\n\n**Base URL**: `https://api.experiment-tracking.example.com/v1`\n\n#### Resources and Endpoints\n\n##### Experiments\n```\nPOST   /experiments                  Create a new experiment\nGET    /experiments                  List all experiments\nGET    /experiments/{experiment_id}  Get experiment details\nDELETE /experiments/{experiment_id}  Archive/delete experiment\n```\n\n##### Runs (nested under experiments)\n```\nPOST   /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs           Start a new run\nGET    /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs           List runs in experiment\nGET    /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}  Get run details\nPATCH  /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}  Update run (end, add final metrics)\nDELETE /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}  Delete/archive run\n```\n\n##### Metrics (nested under runs)\n```\nPOST   /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/metrics     Log metrics (batch)\nGET    /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/metrics     Get all metrics for run\nGET    /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/metrics/{metric_name}  Get specific metric history\n```\n\n##### Parameters\n```\nPOST   /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/params      Log parameters\nGET    /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/params      Get run parameters\n```\n\n##### Artifacts\n```\nPOST   /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/artifacts   Upload artifact\nGET    /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/artifacts   List artifacts\nGET    /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/artifacts/{artifact_id}  Download artifact\n```\n\n##### Tags\n```\nPOST   /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/tags        Add tags\nDELETE /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/tags/{tag}  Remove tag\n```\n\n#### Request/Response Examples\n\n**Create Experiment**\n```http\nPOST /v1/experiments\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  \"name\": \"yolov7-object-detection\",\n  \"description\": \"Hyperparameter tuning for conveyor belt detection\",\n  \"tags\": [\"production\", \"cv-pipeline\"]\n}\n\nResponse 201:\n{\n  \"experiment_id\": \"exp-abc123\",\n  \"name\": \"yolov7-object-detection\",\n  \"created_at\": \"2024-01-15T10:30:00Z\"\n}\n```\n\n**Start Run**\n```http\nPOST /v1/experiments/exp-abc123/runs\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  \"params\": {\n    \"learning_rate\": 0.001,\n    \"batch_size\": 32,\n    \"dropout\": 0.2\n  },\n  \"tags\": [\"random-search\", \"trial-5\"]\n}\n\nResponse 201:\n{\n  \"run_id\": \"run-xyz789\",\n  \"experiment_id\": \"exp-abc123\",\n  \"status\": \"running\",\n  \"start_time\": \"2024-01-15T10:35:00Z\"\n}\n```\n\n**Log Metrics**\n```http\nPOST /v1/experiments/exp-abc123/runs/run-xyz789/metrics\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  \"step\": 100,\n  \"epoch\": 5,\n  \"metrics\": {\n    \"loss\": 0.234,\n    \"accuracy\": 0.876,\n    \"f1_score\": 0.851\n  },\n  \"timestamp\": \"2024-01-15T10:40:00Z\"\n}\n\nResponse 201:\n{ \"logged\": 3 }\n```\n\n**End Run**\n```http\nPATCH /v1/experiments/exp-abc123/runs/run-xyz789\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  \"status\": \"completed\",\n  \"final_metrics\": {\n    \"best_loss\": 0.189,\n    \"best_accuracy\": 0.912\n  }\n}\n\nResponse 200:\n{\n  \"run_id\": \"run-xyz789\",\n  \"status\": \"completed\",\n  \"end_time\": \"2024-01-15T11:00:00Z\",\n  \"duration_seconds\": 1500\n}\n```\n\n**Query Runs**\n```http\nGET /v1/experiments/exp-abc123/runs?status=completed&sort_by=accuracy&order=desc&limit=10\n\nResponse 200:\n{\n  \"runs\": [\n    {\n      \"run_id\": \"run-xyz789\",\n      \"params\": { \"learning_rate\": 0.001, ... },\n      \"final_metrics\": { \"accuracy\": 0.912, ... },\n      \"duration_seconds\": 1500\n    }\n  ],\n  \"total\": 50,\n  \"page\": 1\n}\n```\n\n## Refactoring Plan\n\n### Modules Requiring Modification\n\n| Module | Current Behavior | Required Change |\n|--------|-----------------|-----------------|\n| `module_12.txt` | Direct in-memory `ExperimentTracker` usage | Replace with HTTP client calls to `POST /runs`, `POST /metrics`, `PATCH /runs/{id}` |\n| `module_20.txt` | `HyperparameterRunner` calls `trackers.log_trial()` directly | Inject `ExperimentTrackingClient` that makes HTTP calls instead of direct trait calls |\n| `module_25.txt` | Contains `FileTracker`, `HttpTracker`, `TrackerFactory` | Remove tracker implementations; keep only a thin HTTP client implementing the `ExperimentTracker` trait |\n| `module_54.txt` | `TuningCoordinator` notifies internal observers | Replace internal observer notifications with API calls to log metrics |\n| `module_55.txt` | `ExperimentObserver` receives `ExperimentEvent` internally | Observer implementations call HTTP endpoints instead of local logging |\n| `module_71.txt` | SQLite-backed `ExperimentTracker` persistence | Remove SQLite code; replace with API client calls |\n| `module_76.txt` | `RetrainTrigger` uses `tracker.record()` | Replace with `POST /experiments/{id}/runs` and metric logging calls |\n| `module_77.txt` | `EventBus.emit()` for `TuningEvent` | Add HTTP client that translates `TuningEvent` to API calls |\n| `module_43.txt` | `ModelMonitor` with internal metric tracking | Metrics ingestion should forward to experiment tracking API |\n| `module_48.txt` | `JsonlTracker` writes to local files | Replace with HTTP-based tracker implementation |\n\n### Detailed Refactoring Steps\n\n#### Step 1: Create Thin HTTP Client\n```rust\n// New: src/experiment_tracking_client.rs\npub struct ExperimentTrackingClient {\n    base_url: String,\n    http_client: reqwest::Client,\n}\n\nimpl ExperimentTrackingClient {\n    pub async fn start_run(&self, experiment_id: &str, params: &HyperParams, tags: Vec<String>) -> Result<RunId>;\n    pub async fn log_metrics(&self, experiment_id: &str, run_id: &str, step: usize, metrics: &HashMap<String, f64>) -> Result<()>;\n    pub async fn end_run(&self, experiment_id: &str, run_id: &str, final_metrics: &HashMap<String, f64>) -> Result<()>;\n}\n\n// Implement ExperimentTracker trait for backward compatibility\nimpl ExperimentTracker for ExperimentTrackingClient { /* ... */ }\n```\n\n#### Step 2: Update Configuration\n```toml\n# config.txt changes\n[experiment_tracking]\nenabled = true\nservice_url = \"https://experiment-tracking.internal:8443\"\napi_key_env = \"EXPERIMENT_TRACKING_API_KEY\"\ntimeout_ms = 5000\nretry_attempts = 3\n```\n\n#### Step 3: Modify Consumer Modules\n\n**module_20.txt (HyperparameterRunner)**:\n```rust\n// Before: Vec<Arc<dyn ExperimentTracker>>\n// After: Single HTTP client\npub struct HyperparameterRunner {\n    tuner: Box<dyn Tuner>,\n    bus: Arc<EventBus>,\n    tracking_client: Arc<ExperimentTrackingClient>, // Changed\n}\n```\n\n**module_77.txt (TuningEventHandler observers)**:\n```rust\n// Add new observer that forwards to API\nstruct ApiTrackingObserver {\n    client: Arc<ExperimentTrackingClient>,\n    experiment_id: String,\n    run_id: String,\n}\n\nimpl TuningEventHandler for ApiTrackingObserver {\n    async fn on_event(&self, event: TuningEvent) {\n        match event {\n            TuningEvent::TrialCompleted { trial_id, objective, parameters, .. } => {\n                self.client.log_metrics(&self.experiment_id, &self.run_id, trial_id, &parameters).await;\n            }\n            // ... handle other events\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### Step 4: Remove Deprecated Code\n- Delete `FileTracker`, `LocalFileTracker`, `JsonlTracker` implementations\n- Remove SQLite dependencies from `module_71.txt`\n- Remove in-memory `ExperimentRun` storage from `module_12.txt`\n- Remove `TrackerFactory` (replaced by configuration-based client instantiation)\n\n#### Step 5: Update Tests\n- Mock the HTTP client in unit tests\n- Add integration tests that verify API contract\n- Ensure backward compatibility by keeping the `ExperimentTracker` trait interface\n\n## Summary\n\n- **Primary finding**: The experiment tracking functionality is spread across 7 core modules (module_12, module_20, module_25, module_48, module_55, module_71, module_76) that implement variations of the same capability using Strategy, Factory, and Observer patterns.\n\n- **Key components**:\n  - Core types: `ExperimentTracker` (trait), `ExperimentRun`/`ExperimentRecord`, `Trial`/`TrialRecord`, `TrainingEvent`/`TuningEvent`\n  - Persistence: `FileTracker`, `HttpTracker`, `LocalFileTracker`, `JsonlTracker`, SQLite-backed tracker\n  - Factory: `TrackerFactory`, `TunerFactory`\n  - Observer: `ExperimentObserver`, `TrainingObserver`, `TuningObserver`\n\n- **Architectural pattern**: The codebase uses a consistent Strategy + Factory + Observer pattern combination. The new microservice should expose a RESTful API that maps cleanly to the existing `start_run()`, `log_epoch_metrics()`/`log_trial()`, and `end_run()` operations.\n\n- **Recommendations**:\n  1. Create a unified `ExperimentTrackingClient` implementing the existing `ExperimentTracker` trait to minimize consumer code changes\n  2. The microservice should implement the proposed REST API covering experiments, runs, metrics, parameters, artifacts, and tags\n  3. Consumer modules (module_43, module_54, module_76, module_77, module_20) need refactoring to inject the HTTP client instead of local tracker implementations\n  4. Consider maintaining the event bus (`EventBus` from utils.txt) internally but have a dedicated observer that forwards events to the microservice API\n  5. SQLite and file-based persistence should be moved entirely to the microservice, not the monolith\n",

Option<SystemTime>,\n    pub metrics: HashMap<String, f64>,\n    pub tags: Vec<String>,\n}\n\npub struct ExperimentTracker {\n    state: Arc<RwLock<HashMap<Uuid, ExperimentRun>>>,\n    broadcaster: Uuid { /* ... */ }\n\n    pub async fn log_epoch_metrics(\n        &self,\n        run_id: Uuid,\n        epoch: usize,\n        metrics: HashMap<String, f64>,\n    ) -> Result<(), TunerError> { /* ... */ }\n\n    pub async fn end_run(\n        &self,\n        run_id: Uuid,\n        final_metrics: HashMap<String, f64>,\n    ) -> Result<(), TunerError> { /* ... */ }\n\n    pub async fn get_run(&self, run_id: Uuid) -> Option<ExperimentRun> { /* ... */ }\n}\n```\n\n### ExperimentTracker Trait Definition\n```rust\n// File: /app/project/src/module_25.txt\n// Lines: 80-83\n#[async_trait]\npub trait ExperimentTracker: Send + Sync {\n    async fn log_trial(&self, trial: &Trial) -> Result<(), OrchestratorError>;\n}\n```\n\n### SQLite-backed Experiment Persistence\n```rust\n// File: /app/project/src/module_71.txt\n// Lines: 246-258, 291-308\npub struct ExperimentTracker {\n    db_path: PathBuf,\n    conn: Connection,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct ExperimentRecord {\n    pub id: i64,\n    pub timestamp: DateTime<Utc>,\n    pub tuner_name: String,\n    pub params: HyperParams,\n    pub metric: f64,\n}\n\nimpl ExperimentTracker {\n    pub fn log_record(&self, tuner_name: &str, params: &HyperParams, metric: f64) -> Result<i64> { /* ... */ }\n    pub fn all_records(&self) -> Result<Vec<ExperimentRecord>> { /* ... */ }\n}\n```\n\n### Observer Pattern for Experiment Events\n```rust\n// File: /app/project/src/module_55.txt\n// Lines: 85-110\npub enum ExperimentEvent<M: Trainable> {\n    TrialStarted(M::HyperParams),\n    TrialCompleted(TrialRecord<M>),\n    TuningFinished(Option<TrialRecord<M>>),\n}\n\npub trait ExperimentObserver<M: Trainable>: Send + Sync {\n    fn on_event(&self, event: ExperimentEvent<M>);\n}\n```\n\n### Configuration Reference to Experiment Tracking\n```toml\n# File: /app/project/src/config.txt\n# Lines: 97-104\n[model_ops]\ndefault_model        = \"yolov7\"\nhyperparameter_tuning = true\ntuning_backend       = \"optuna\"\ntuning_trials        = 50\nexperiment_tracking_uri = \"http://mlflow:5000\"\n```\n\n### Tuning Consumer Using ExperimentTracker\n```rust\n// File: /app/project/src/module_20.txt\n// Lines: 317-370\npub struct HyperparameterRunner {\n    tuner: Box<dyn Tuner>,\n    bus: Arc<EventBus>,\n    trackers: Vec<Arc<dyn ExperimentTracker>>,\n}\n\nimpl HyperparameterRunner {\n    pub fn run<Evaluate>(&mut self, mut eval_fn: Evaluate) -> Result<()>\n    where\n        Evaluate: FnMut(&Candidate) -> Result<f64>,\n    {\n        loop {\n            let cand = match self.tuner.next_candidate() { /* ... */ };\n            let score = eval_fn(&cand)?;\n            let evt = TrialFinishedEvent { /* ... */ };\n            self.bus.dispatch(evt.clone());\n            for t in &self.trackers {\n                if let Err(e) = t.log_trial(&evt) {\n                    log::warn!(\"Experiment-tracker error: {e}\");\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### 1. Core Component Identification\n\nThe experiment tracking functionality is distributed across multiple modules following a consistent architectural pattern:\n\n| Module | Primary Responsibility | Key Types |\n|--------|----------------------|-----------|\n| `module_12.txt` | In-memory experiment run management | `ExperimentTracker`, `ExperimentRun`, `TrainingEvent` |\n| `module_25.txt` | Tracker trait and factory | `ExperimentTracker` (trait), `FileTracker`, `HttpTracker`, `TrackerFactory` |\n| `module_20.txt` | Tracker trait and file-based logging | `ExperimentTracker` (trait), `LocalFileTracker`, `TrialFinishedEvent` |\n| `module_71.txt` | SQLite-backed persistence | `ExperimentTracker`, `ExperimentRecord` |\n| `module_55.txt` | Observer pattern for experiments | `ExperimentEvent`, `ExperimentObserver`, `TrialRecord` |\n| `module_48.txt` | JSONL file-based observer | `TuningObserver`, `JsonlTracker` |\n| `module_76.txt` | Monitoring integration | `ExperimentTracker` (for retraining logs) |\n\n### 2. Dependency Analysis\n\n#### Internal Dependencies (what core modules depend on):\n\n| Dependency | Modules Using It | Purpose |\n|------------|-----------------|---------|\n| `config.txt` | All trackers | `experiment_tracking_uri`, backend selection |\n| `utils.txt` | All modules | `AppConfig`, `event_bus`, error types, `ScopedTimer` |\n| `constants.txt` | Feature-flagged modules | `HYPERPARAM_TUNING` feature flag |\n| `serde`, `serde_json` | All trackers | Serialization of trials and metrics |\n| `tokio`, `async_trait` | Async trackers | Async I/O operations |\n| `rusqlite` | `module_71.txt` | SQLite persistence |\n| `reqwest` | `module_25.txt` | HTTP-based remote tracking |\n\n#### External Consumers (modules that use experiment tracking):\n\n| Consumer Module | How It Uses Experiment Tracking |\n|-----------------|--------------------------------|\n| `module_77.txt` | `EventBus` emits `TuningEvent` for experiment logging |\n| `module_54.txt` | `TuningCoordinator` feeds metrics to observers |\n| `module_43.txt` | `ModelMonitor` triggers retraining with metric logging |\n| `module_76.txt` | `RetrainTrigger` records experiments after tuning |\n| `module_20.txt` | `HyperparameterRunner` logs trials via tracker list |\n| `module_53.txt` | Tuning strategies log results |\n| `module_23.txt` | Factory creates tuners that integrate with trackers |\n\n### 3. Architectural Patterns Used\n\n1. **Strategy Pattern**: Multiple tuning algorithms (`GridSearchTuner`, `RandomSearchTuner`, `BayesianTuner`) implement common `Tuner`/`HyperparameterTuner` traits\n2. **Factory Pattern**: `TrackerFactory`, `TunerFactory` instantiate concrete implementations at runtime\n3. **Observer Pattern**: `ExperimentObserver`, `TrainingObserver`, `TuningObserver` receive notifications about trial events\n4. **Repository Pattern**: `ExperimentTracker` abstracts persistence (file, HTTP, SQLite backends)\n\n## Proposed Service API\n\n### RESTful API Design for Experiment Tracking Microservice\n\n**Base URL**: `https://api.experiment-tracking.example.com/v1`\n\n#### Resources and Endpoints\n\n##### Experiments\n```\nPOST   /experiments                  Create a new experiment\nGET    /experiments                  List all experiments\nGET    /experiments/{experiment_id}  Get experiment details\nDELETE /experiments/{experiment_id}  Archive/delete experiment\n```\n\n##### Runs (nested under experiments)\n```\nPOST   /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs           Start a new run\nGET    /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs           List runs in experiment\nGET    /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}  Get run details\nPATCH  /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}  Update run (end, add final metrics)\nDELETE /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}  Delete/archive run\n```\n\n##### Metrics (nested under runs)\n```\nPOST   /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/metrics     Log metrics (batch)\nGET    /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/metrics     Get all metrics for run\nGET    /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/metrics/{metric_name}  Get specific metric history\n```\n\n##### Parameters\n```\nPOST   /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/params      Log parameters\nGET    /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/params      Get run parameters\n```\n\n##### Artifacts\n```\nPOST   /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/artifacts   Upload artifact\nGET    /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/artifacts   List artifacts\nGET    /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/artifacts/{artifact_id}  Download artifact\n```\n\n##### Tags\n```\nPOST   /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/tags        Add tags\nDELETE /experiments/{experiment_id}/runs/{run_id}/tags/{tag}  Remove tag\n```\n\n#### Request/Response Examples\n\n**Create Experiment**\n```http\nPOST /v1/experiments\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  \"name\": \"yolov7-object-detection\",\n  \"description\": \"Hyperparameter tuning for conveyor belt detection\",\n  \"tags\": [\"production\", \"cv-pipeline\"]\n}\n\nResponse 201:\n{\n  \"experiment_id\": \"exp-abc123\",\n  \"name\": \"yolov7-object-detection\",\n  \"created_at\": \"2024-01-15T10:30:00Z\"\n}\n```\n\n**Start Run**\n```http\nPOST /v1/experiments/exp-abc123/runs\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  \"params\": {\n    \"learning_rate\": 0.001,\n    \"batch_size\": 32,\n    \"dropout\": 0.2\n  },\n  \"tags\": [\"random-search\", \"trial-5\"]\n}\n\nResponse 201:\n{\n  \"run_id\": \"run-xyz789\",\n  \"experiment_id\": \"exp-abc123\",\n  \"status\": \"running\",\n  \"start_time\": \"2024-01-15T10:35:00Z\"\n}\n```\n\n**Log Metrics**\n```http\nPOST /v1/experiments/exp-abc123/runs/run-xyz789/metrics\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  \"step\": 100,\n  \"epoch\": 5,\n  \"metrics\": {\n    \"loss\": 0.234,\n    \"accuracy\": 0.876,\n    \"f1_score\": 0.851\n  },\n  \"timestamp\": \"2024-01-15T10:40:00Z\"\n}\n\nResponse 201:\n{ \"logged\": 3 }\n```\n\n**End Run**\n```http\nPATCH /v1/experiments/exp-abc123/runs/run-xyz789\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  \"status\": \"completed\",\n  \"final_metrics\": {\n    \"best_loss\": 0.189,\n    \"best_accuracy\": 0.912\n  }\n}\n\nResponse 200:\n{\n  \"run_id\": \"run-xyz789\",\n  \"status\": \"completed\",\n  \"end_time\": \"2024-01-15T11:00:00Z\",\n  \"duration_seconds\": 1500\n}\n```\n\n**Query Runs**\n```http\nGET /v1/experiments/exp-abc123/runs?status=completed&sort_by=accuracy&order=desc&limit=10\n\nResponse 200:\n{\n  \"runs\": [\n    {\n      \"run_id\": \"run-xyz789\",\n      \"params\": { \"learning_rate\": 0.001, ... },\n      \"final_metrics\": { \"accuracy\": 0.912, ... },\n      \"duration_seconds\": 1500\n    }\n  ],\n  \"total\": 50,\n  \"page\": 1\n}\n```\n\n## Refactoring Plan\n\n### Modules Requiring Modification\n\n| Module | Current Behavior | Required Change |\n|--------|-----------------|-----------------|\n| `module_12.txt` | Direct in-memory `ExperimentTracker` usage | Replace with HTTP client calls to `POST /runs`, `POST /metrics`, `PATCH /runs/{id}` |\n| `module_20.txt` | `HyperparameterRunner` calls `trackers.log_trial()` directly | Inject `ExperimentTrackingClient` that makes HTTP calls instead of direct trait calls |\n| `module_25.txt` | Contains `FileTracker`, `HttpTracker`, `TrackerFactory` | Remove tracker implementations; keep only a thin HTTP client implementing the `ExperimentTracker` trait |\n| `module_54.txt` | `TuningCoordinator` notifies internal observers | Replace internal observer notifications with API calls to log metrics |\n| `module_55.txt` | `ExperimentObserver` receives `ExperimentEvent` internally | Observer implementations call HTTP endpoints instead of local logging |\n| `module_71.txt` | SQLite-backed `ExperimentTracker` persistence | Remove SQLite code; replace with API client calls |\n| `module_76.txt` | `RetrainTrigger` uses `tracker.record()` | Replace with `POST /experiments/{id}/runs` and metric logging calls |\n| `module_77.txt` | `EventBus.emit()` for `TuningEvent` | Add HTTP client that translates `TuningEvent` to API calls |\n| `module_43.txt` | `ModelMonitor` with internal metric tracking | Metrics ingestion should forward to experiment tracking API |\n| `module_48.txt` | `JsonlTracker` writes to local files | Replace with HTTP-based tracker implementation |\n\n### Detailed Refactoring Steps\n\n#### Step 1: Create Thin HTTP Client\n```rust\n// New: src/experiment_tracking_client.rs\npub struct ExperimentTrackingClient {\n    base_url: String,\n    http_client: reqwest::Client,\n}\n\nimpl ExperimentTrackingClient {\n    pub async fn start_run(&self, experiment_id: &str, params: &HyperParams, tags: Vec<String>) -> Result<RunId>;\n    pub async fn log_metrics(&self, experiment_id: &str, run_id: &str, step: usize, metrics: &HashMap<String, f64>) -> Result<()>;\n    pub async fn end_run(&self, experiment_id: &str, run_id: &str, final_metrics: &HashMap<String, f64>) -> Result<()>;\n}\n\n// Implement ExperimentTracker trait for backward compatibility\nimpl ExperimentTracker for ExperimentTrackingClient { /* ... */ }\n```\n\n#### Step 2: Update Configuration\n```toml\n# config.txt changes\n[experiment_tracking]\nenabled = true\nservice_url = \"https://experiment-tracking.internal:8443\"\napi_key_env = \"EXPERIMENT_TRACKING_API_KEY\"\ntimeout_ms = 5000\nretry_attempts = 3\n```\n\n#### Step 3: Modify Consumer Modules\n\n**module_20.txt (HyperparameterRunner)**:\n```rust\n// Before: Vec<Arc<dyn ExperimentTracker>>\n// After: Single HTTP client\npub struct HyperparameterRunner {\n    tuner: Box<dyn Tuner>,\n    bus: Arc<EventBus>,\n    tracking_client: Arc<ExperimentTrackingClient>, // Changed\n}\n```\n\n**module_77.txt (TuningEventHandler observers)**:\n```rust\n// Add new observer that forwards to API\nstruct ApiTrackingObserver {\n    client: Arc<ExperimentTrackingClient>,\n    experiment_id: String,\n    run_id: String,\n}\n\nimpl TuningEventHandler for ApiTrackingObserver {\n    async fn on_event(&self, event: TuningEvent) {\n        match event {\n            TuningEvent::TrialCompleted { trial_id, objective, parameters, .. } => {\n                self.client.log_metrics(&self.experiment_id, &self.run_id, trial_id, &parameters).await;\n            }\n            // ... handle other events\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### Step 4: Remove Deprecated Code\n- Delete `FileTracker`, `LocalFileTracker`, `JsonlTracker` implementations\n- Remove SQLite dependencies from `module_71.txt`\n- Remove in-memory `ExperimentRun` storage from `module_12.txt`\n- Remove `TrackerFactory` (replaced by configuration-based client instantiation)\n\n#### Step 5: Update Tests\n- Mock the HTTP client in unit tests\n- Add integration tests that verify API contract\n- Ensure backward compatibility by keeping the `ExperimentTracker` trait interface\n\n## Summary\n\n- **Primary finding**: The experiment tracking functionality is spread across 7 core modules (module_12, module_20, module_25, module_48, module_55, module_71, module_76) that implement variations of the same capability using Strategy, Factory, and Observer patterns.\n\n- **Key components**:\n  - Core types: `ExperimentTracker` (trait), `ExperimentRun`/`ExperimentRecord`, `Trial`/`TrialRecord`, `TrainingEvent`/`TuningEvent`\n  - Persistence: `FileTracker`, `HttpTracker`, `LocalFileTracker`, `JsonlTracker`, SQLite-backed tracker\n  - Factory: `TrackerFactory`, `TunerFactory`\n  - Observer: `ExperimentObserver`, `TrainingObserver`, `TuningObserver`\n\n- **Architectural pattern**: The codebase uses a consistent Strategy + Factory + Observer pattern combination. The new microservice should expose a RESTful API that maps cleanly to the existing `start_run()`, `log_epoch_metrics()`/`log_trial()`, and `end_run()` operations.\n\n- **Recommendations**:\n  1. Create a unified `ExperimentTrackingClient` implementing the existing `ExperimentTracker` trait to minimize consumer code changes\n  2. The microservice should implement the proposed REST API covering experiments, runs, metrics, parameters, artifacts, and tags\n  3. Consumer modules (module_43, module_54, module_76, module_77, module_20) need refactoring to inject the HTTP client instead of local tracker implementations\n  4. Consider maintaining the event bus (`EventBus` from utils.txt) internally but have a dedicated observer that forwards events to the microservice API\n  5. SQLite and file-based persistence should be moved entirely to the microservice, not the monolith\n",
